lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘嗣堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省济南市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十六岁。退休前原是济南市钢铁总公司设备制造公司机动科科长兼技术工程师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，刘嗣堂夫妻在济南天桥区桑梓店集市赶集向民众讲法轮功真相、发放法轮功真相资料，被天桥区公安分局桑梓店派出所警察抓捕，后因年龄大当天被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，济南市天桥区检察院以刘嗣堂有所谓的“前科”（曾被非法判刑五年半）对他进行批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，刘嗣堂被济南市天桥区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘淑芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西大同法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，大同市刘淑芳因给当权者寄信反映法轮功学员被迫害的事实，遭到公检法部门的打击报复，一周后被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。这已是刘淑芳第三次被迫害。第一次是因依法起诉江泽民迫害法轮功，遭到打击报复，行政拘留十五日。第二次是因依信访条例给当权者寄信，反映法轮功学员被基层公检法人员绑架、滥用职权枉法追诉，而被打击报复，行政拘留十五日，这次依然是因给当权者寄信，在家门口被监控绑架。这一次直接判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘淑亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，原贵阳市铁路客运段退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，贺云杰和刘淑娅为了帮助市民了解法轮功，发放法轮功资料，期间被人恶告。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，贺云杰和刘淑娅分别被贵阳铁路公安、南明区分局国保、二戈寨派出所警察抓捕、抄家，被关押到五当区三江看守所。被关押了<span lang="EN-US">162</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日分别被南宁区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘万胜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，辽宁锦州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午十点钟左右，刘万胜在锦州站前汽车站讲法轮功时，被锦铁派出所警察抓捕。当日刘万胜的租房处被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初被锦州凌海市法院视频庭审。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，家属被告知刘万胜遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘卫国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，北京市丰台区人，化名刘于谦，北京源佳科技公司职员，自由信仰者，新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市常驻居民，“耶和华见证人”教派信徒，前重庆会众长老，前新疆伊犁会众长老，库尔勒会众长老，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，自从在北京基督某教派“耶和华见证人”受洗以来，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被派往重庆举行传教，后被安立（任命）为重庆会众长老；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又前往新疆伊犁市做伊犁会众长老；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又被任命库尔勒会众长老；因曾大力发展教会信徒，举办会众参加圣经培训及举办<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多次家庭聚会，从而引起库尔勒市当局关注；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因曾两次参加“耶和华见证人”香港分部的区域大会，后又在库尔勒楼兰世家组织聚会，随被库尔勒市民宗委查处；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，因曾到韩国参加过区域大会，遂再遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，与多人被巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市警方悉数抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪 ”转正式被捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人被库尔勒市检察院提起公诉，指控其所属教会与正统基督教教义不符，宣传“政治中性”，要求信徒“不履行国家宪法，不参加爱国主义教育，不服兵役，不入党，不如团，不升国旗，不唱国歌，不向国旗敬礼”等，同时又打着基督教旗号，积极发展组织成员，多次组织、提供场所进行聚会，故而触犯了政府法律规定，属于参与邪教的违法行为；截至目前，其具体信息缺详，至今未审待判。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘文廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省沧州市盐山县法轮功学员。）杨月亮、刘文廷在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日给人安装卫星电视接收器（据称可收看新唐人电视台）时遭圣佛镇派出所警察抓捕，后被非法关押在盐山县看守所。杨月亮被非法关押近一个月后遭盐山县检察院非法批捕。刘文廷被非法刑拘一个月时遭勒索保证金后“取保”回家。取保半年后，又被“监视居住”近一年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，刘文廷再次遭关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，杨月亮遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；刘文廷被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">刘湘菊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省沈阳市辽中区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刘湘菊在向村民发放法轮功真相台历时，被辽中区公安局警察绑架。第二天，辽中区城郊派出所警察去她家抄家，在她家无人的情况下，私自掠走了她丈夫打工挣来的九千元现金。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刘湘菊女士被辽中区法院非法庭审，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下达判决书，被非法判刑七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘学荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省烟台市牟平区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。刘学荣老人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午在牟平区集贸市场发法轮大法资料，被便衣警察绑架，随后被关押到烟台市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，牟平区公检法机构秘密对老人判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被关押到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，家住武穴市城区，现在被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刘艳峰刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳华<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南周口市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被中共劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，之后多次被骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，刘艳华及丈夫刘冲还有到她家串门的法轮功学员杜子良，被河南省周口市公安局荷花分局四、五个警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年元月，刘艳华被河南周口市川汇区法院第三刑事庭判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，家属毫不知情。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生于<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年，湖北荆门公民，人权捍卫者。原是荆门市一间银行的职员。刘艳丽是因网上公布与国保的对话记录，因言获罪<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日遭刑事拘留，罪名竟然是“诽谤罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日又被逮捕。共被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日取保获释。刘艳丽主要做帮助抗战老兵工作，是一名追求民主自由人士，网上言论较多，是一位政治异见人士。刘艳丽<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午开始被荆门公安国保传唤。后获知刘艳丽遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘艳丽女士因言获罪，被荆门市东宝区法院以寻衅滋事罪判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘尧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东河源市知名维权律师。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生。刘尧是自学成为律师，曾专门受理农民与开发商及地方官员间的“征地”纠纷案件。刘尧第一次出名是在</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2007</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，当时他因参与一场农村抗议活动被拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2008</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，刘尧被判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。此前，刘尧所代表的村民与一个水电站的保安人员对峙，检方称，有价值</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元人民币的建筑材料在对峙中被毁坏。对这个情节较轻的案件，判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年的结果在中国法律界引起抗议。法律人士纷纷为他辩护。当时是李方平和浦志强等维权律师代理他进行了一系列上诉，最终使刘尧的刑期减为</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月监禁。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月下旬，刘尧实名向中共广东省纪检委举报，并在网上发文，指河源市委书记何忠友非法支持广东康泉十八国际生态健康旅游城有限公司违法占用农地，包括基本农田的项目，修建高尔夫球场。中国的法规（基本农田保护条例第</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">条）明确规定任何单位和个人不得改变或者占用基本农田。同时，刘尧还向纪检委举报当时河源市公安局局长彭定邦毫无理由地停止调查</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名商人销售假冒著名韶关钢铁公司品牌的钢材，敦促纪委以涉嫌受贿的问题调查彭定邦。没多久，于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，刘尧被河源市公安局源城分局以涉嫌“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”（后撤销指控）和“敲诈勒索罪”刑事拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，刘尧被广东河源市源城区法院以“敲诈勒索罪”、“诈骗罪”和“收买被拐卖的儿童罪”数罪并罚，判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑，罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">140</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元人民币（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">221,000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">美元）。刘尧认为，他被起诉和定罪，是因为他长期举报河源市党政官员的贪腐行为，而遭到河源市</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多名纪检、检察、法院官员“帮助腐败党政高官报复陷害”。后上诉、申诉均遭驳回。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2036</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘银凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁凤城市红旗镇法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。<a name="_Hlk52322012">刘银凤</a><span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日去黄旗赶集买鸡蛋，回家途中被红旗派出所抓捕抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被凤城法院庭审，后获悉刘银凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省抚顺市清原县<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的法轮功学员，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在贴“法轮大法好”粘贴时被警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日遭清原县法院庭审，后被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年的一天，经人介绍刘玉开始学炼法轮功。刘玉曾患有胃癌，因修炼法轮功才得以康复。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，刘玉用自己的亲身经历向民众讲述大法的美好，揭穿中共喉舌媒体谎言。为此刘玉多次遭绑架、关押：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年冬天被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日再次被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被绑架，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；回家不到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘玉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日再次被绑架，后又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">刘玉霞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：女，现年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，河南省平顶山市人，原在市政府物价局工作，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功遭迫害，曾被多次送“洗脑班”、拘留，甚至被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并在新乡女子监狱服刑，遭非人虐待，同时被单位开除，无任何生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午七点多，刘玉霞在路上发邀请函，请人们旁听法轮功信仰者穆亚东的庭审，结果又被光明路派出所抓捕，后关押到平顶山宝丰县看守所。由于刘玉霞不报姓名，直到下午七点，派出所根据手纹用技术手段才查出刘玉霞的身份和住址。晚上八点，其家被查抄，搜走法轮功书籍多本、未发出去的邀请函及几个真相光盘等。随后，她就被刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘玉霞被平顶山市新华区法院一审重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千。其不服上诉，后经平顶山市中级法院不公开审理，依然维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日她已被送往到河南省新乡女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52326998"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘玉英</span></b></a><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省清原县法轮功学员。辽宁省清原县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，马凤菊、刘玉英在清原易和小区发放法轮功资料，被清原镇河南派出所警察王东等人抓捕，被关押在抚顺看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日开庭，未当庭宣判。后获悉，马凤菊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，刘玉英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘永泽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者等群体维权诉讼代理人，民间公益组织“长沙富能”<span lang="EN-US">NGO</span>成员，中国在押政治犯。曾多年从事公益维权活动，代理过多起乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者维权诉讼等案件，深受弱势群体欢迎；近年来，因从事公益维权活动且与海外人道服务机构多有来往，随遭中共当局警觉与严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，因在推特上转发同情香港「反送中」抗议行动的言论以及自由亚洲电台对香港反送中游行的报导，随于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方突然跨境从广州市其办公室带走，并被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；审讯期间，多被问及其在长沙富能所做工作内容、资金何来、与哪些海外机构有染或合作及其近期发推特所涉内容等详情；据悉，其事先委托代理律师向长沙市国家安全局了解详情遭拒，仅告知被控涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”，原因不明，疑与香港正在进行的反送中风潮有关；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，获知长沙市国家安全局已向长沙市检察院申请对其进行逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。已遭起诉，案件已在法院，目前尚未开庭。被强迫辞退律师，接受官派律师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月已经开庭，信息遭当局封锁。目前被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘志峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘志峰等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，刘志峰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘中花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省莱西市法轮功学员。刘中花被莱西市法院非法判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被送往山东省女子监狱。刘中花曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。此次被非法判刑，是因为她给警察讲真相而被劫持构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘中花到日庄镇派出所给警察讲述法轮大法，警察将刘中花扣押并送入大牢。次刘中花被抓，她家人的一切权利全被剥夺，其家人直到收到山东省女子监狱的信才知道刘中花被判刑并被送进监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柳德玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省荆门市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，曾多次遭到迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月历经<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年残酷迫害后，从范家台监狱黑窝回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在讲法轮功时又被绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，荆门市东宝区法院庭审柳德玉，历时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分钟。当场未宣布刑期。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获知，柳德玉被冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被转到湖北沙洋范家台监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柳秋生：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西省九江市法轮功学员，都昌县人。柳秋生原来在都昌县调查队从事统计调查工作（公务员）。因为坚持信仰真善忍，遭迫害被开除公职，没有生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，柳秋生遭抓捕。非法抄家时抄收现金六万元还有存款和五万美元存单。构陷编造的罪名是“里通外国”，其实是柳秋生家中房屋拆迁款，柳秋生在银行的同学帮助存了美元存单，取不了，美元只是利息高点，这笔钱是留给儿子读大学用的。当局给柳秋生强按的罪名是“里通外国”，<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被九江市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳全春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1975</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，辽宁省大石桥市旗口镇农民，法轮功学员。辽宁大石桥市法轮功学员柳全春、史庆秀夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭营口市站前区法院在看守所庭审，两位律师出庭为他们进行无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，法官赵丹就下了判决：分别判刑柳全春和史庆秀<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，并没收所有扣押的物品。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省绵阳市法轮功学员。柳涛女士，大学毕业后在深圳工作。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七月江泽民迫害法轮功后，她讲法轮功真相，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在广东三水劳教所因炼功被每个犯人各抽<span lang="EN-US">30</span>鞭子等残暴迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日在绵阳市再次被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，在四川女子监狱遭吊在钢管上毒打，被强制戴手铐脚镣、关小号、不准睡觉等酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，绵阳市法轮功学员柳涛与三台县法轮功学员邓成开到三台县芦溪镇去买东西被抓捕。柳涛被关押在绵阳市看守所，邓成开被关押在三台县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，柳涛、邓承开被绵阳市三台县法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金二千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢凤花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">青岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十五岁，家住青岛市西海岸新区胶南办事处象沟头村。在中共迫害法轮功持续至今近二十年中，卢凤花曾被判刑八年，在济南监狱被迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在家包粽子，被胶南派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被胶南检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被黄岛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢向辉</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：陕西咸阳网民陈鹰军、王兴杰等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>人因在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传播涉及政治的内容于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被咸阳市秦都区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半有期徒刑。判决书指控他们通过<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群有组织地传播“涉及政治的谣言”，攻击政府、党和国家领导人。被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名陕西咸阳网民分别是：陈鹰军、王兴杰、卢向辉、刘芗、周昱、朱远亮、李好轩、徐海波、李泰营、周福评、潘建、廖焕华、武刚。其中，陈鹰军在庭审中只高喊口号，不做辩护，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b>王兴杰、卢向辉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日；</b>刘芗、周昱、朱远亮、李好轩、徐海波、李泰营、周福评、潘建等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日；廖焕华、武刚被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。廖焕华、武刚已获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢永良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南岳阳市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，卢永良在家中与几位法轮功学员一起读法轮大法著作。被警察入户抓捕，并抄家。电脑、打印机、刻录机、大法书籍、真相资料等私人物品被警察抄走。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。卢永良被关押一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被湖南省平江县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，没收电脑、打印机、刻录机、装订机等。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陆建华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，上海市人，前中国最高层核心智囊之一，第二届“北京市十大杰出青年”，曾任中国社会科学院社会学研究所研究员、公共政策研究中心副主任，中央电视台特约评论员和重庆市渝北区副区长等职，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，因陆续为香港记者程翔提供<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余篇稿件，其中<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月所提供的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>篇文章内容被中共视为涉及“国家绝密资料”，遂于<span lang="EN-US"> 2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被国家安全局秘密拘捕；后经秘密审判，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市第二中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 20</span>年；其上诉坚称自己被冤，均被驳回。目前在北京市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆建荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏讨薪农民工、维权公民。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年先后两次于六四敏感日因转发中国公民及国际友人在驻美中国大使馆门口举行纪念“六<span lang="EN-US">.</span>四”活动的图片遭到警方传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被江苏警方跨省抓捕，涉嫌“非法买卖枪支弹药罪”，至今不被释放，被刑拘于泰兴市看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆祚钰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">福建失地农民、维权人士。陆祚钰是福建省屏南县古汾镇长汾村人，一家<span lang="EN-US">8</span>口人共十余亩耕地，靠种植蘑菇和养猪的收入维持生活。到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，全家的耕地被政府动用暴力强行征用，一家人还多人被政府雇佣的征地人员打伤，报警公安不予理睬，陆祚钰为此走访各级政府，反映地方政府违法征用耕地的行为，结果是屡屡遭到打击报复，甚至被判刑入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底因北京上访被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被行政拘留九天期满，于当日上午八点被公安以“寻衅滋事”立即传唤，并于当天下午三点以口袋罪“寻衅滋事”升级为刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，又遭正式批捕、起诉。羁押于宁德看守所。陆祚钰遭当局构陷寻衅滋事罪案将于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午九点在柘荣县法院第一法庭开庭审理，由纪中久律师代理，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">鲁•贡确嘉措：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海省黄南州尖扎县拉莫德钦寺僧人，因写书记录流亡印度觐见达赖喇嘛尊者的经历，近日第二次遭当局带走，目前与外界失联。鲁•贡确嘉措将自己翻越雪山、赴印拜见达赖喇嘛尊者的过程，写成名为《五十四天》的书籍。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年年底完稿后被警方约谈，带到黄南州国安局非法扣留审问长达一周之久，并被警告不得出版该书。获释后不满一个月，贡确嘉措再次被当局约谈，目前与外界失联。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，黄南州统战部打电话约谈，他回复说等雪停了后再去，结果下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分左右，两名黄南州安全局的人员将他带走，之后便没有了任何消息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鲁扬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，本名张桂祺，网名“鲁西狂徒”，山东省莘县人，著名诗人。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年开始诗歌文学创作活动，创办“扬子宛诗社”，并主编出版《扬子宛诗刊》。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年创办“中国当代诗歌论坛”，出版主编《中国当代诗歌》刊物。二年后“中国当代诗论坛”被封。期间开始在《星星》、《诗选刊》等国内著名诗歌刊物上发表诗歌。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年创办“中国自由文化论坛”，因颇有影响而被迫多次关停，后移入外网“自由中国”网站，最后又移入博讯网站。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因自由写作被迫于聊城外国学校辞职，后妻子工作也受到牵连，一起离开山东，南方谋生，此间由诗歌创作转入文化自由写作，大量作品发表于国内各大网站，并被海外多家网站转载。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与“零八宪章”签署，夫妻工作再次受到影响，双双失业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，为支持入狱的本会前会长刘晓波而入独立中文笔会。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年受“茉莉花运动”影响，再次失业并遭遣返回山东老家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因举牌声援批评毛泽东遭解职的山东广播电视台特约评论员邓相超教授，在邓教授所在的济南建筑大学遭到暴徒殴打，受到中外媒体关注，同时也成为有关部门重点监控对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年创办“中国诗人大讲堂——文殊书院”，继续从事自由文化传播事业。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方带走，下落不明近两个星期，后被聊城市公安局以“涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪”宣布刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日已被秘密开庭，家属竟然被封锁，对此一无所知。关押于聊城市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">栾凝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">，男，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，大学文化，原来在宁夏劳动人事厅工作，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功前，是宁夏法轮功辅导站副站长（义务教功）。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，栾凝到兴庆区一邮政储蓄所邮寄信件。栾凝离开后，被该所人员以信件涉及法轮功内容向派出所报警，并将信件交给派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，栾凝上班时在家门口被抓捕。宁夏银川市中级法院在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下达判决书，对栾凝判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛迪嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区索县若达乡索卡村人，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Lodoe Gyamtso</span>，西藏民间舞蹈艺术家，藏族人权捍卫者，异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初，曾因其姐、妹二人在一场车祸中被司机撞死及遭到谋杀，而当时的那曲地方法院竟枉法以该司机为亲共藏人为由，判其“无罪”；同年晚些时候，两人在村庄市场相遇，随发生争执冲突，冲突中为了躲避司机方对其的两次射杀，其被迫自卫，刺伤了司机，致使该司机虽送医院仍最终死亡；针此，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被西藏那曲中级法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后送拉萨市扎奇监狱服刑；服刑期间，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又曾因在扎奇监狱带领狱友高喊“西藏独立”，“中国退出西藏”，“祈愿达赖喇嘛尊者长久住世”，“六百万藏人要团结”等口号进行抗议，并散发手写传单<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多份，在遭受审讯及酷刑折磨<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月之后，被西藏当局决定处于死刑，后在联合国及国际特赦等组织的干预下，才未对其施行处决，但又加刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并被转至拉萨市曲水监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其终获刑满获释，但又被软禁在家<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因公开谴责中共西藏当局强迫居住在西藏巴青县、索县和比如县的藏人中共八一建军节时穿珍贵野兽皮毛饰品（此为传统藏人服饰，但藏人已从<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年始自愿放弃穿戴该饰品）和表演歌舞等，并将其认同的达赖喇嘛提出的解决西藏问题的“中间道路”和“和平区”等概念，以及对佛教姻缘和非暴力原则重要性的感悟和认识，让其妻噶吉拍录视频，广为传播，而遭致当局的仇视与严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又曾因公开反对中共当局强令除在西藏之外，在藏区其他各地寺院里学习的僧侣、尼师必须限期返回索县和比如县等，否则其家属将面临遭监禁和接受禁止挖虫草处罚等非人道作法（挖虫草是当地藏人经济收入的最主要来源），随再遭当局拘押，并关押在比如县监狱中，后因健康状况不佳，才准予释放；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因在拉萨市布达拉宫前举行抗议活动，并在网上发视频，宣称自己正在发起一场“世界和平运动”，引起海外流亡藏人广泛热议，随被那曲地区索县警方再次拘捕，并被以“国家机密案”论处；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其被西藏自治区那曲县中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”再次重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前在拉萨市扎什监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛米（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，本名嘉央，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡三村人，阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，格尔登寺闻思辩经学院般若班学员，非暴力追求者，藏族知名作家，中国在押良心犯。因长期在藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺闻思辩经学院般若班学习，且爱撰写发表、出版许多相关文章及书籍（如《弥漫的橙黄烟雾》等），从而成为海内外藏人区域知名的僧人作家，又因平素崇尚非暴力，致力于藏母语保护宣传，深受藏人及境内外网友喜爱；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被阿坝县警方突然秘密抓捕，罪由不清，自此失联；其家人、亲友及寺庙僧侣等均感震惊、担忧，其同为作家的友人疑称可能与其发表、撰写了关乎西藏命运的文章，尤其从事了环保活动有关；后知其被当局转正式逮捕，并关押于汶川县看守所；羁押期间，其饱受酷刑折磨，并在庭审前曾被利诱，要求为官方做事，称其若答应则可为其家人提供经济援助，并准其出境旅游等，若不答应则将重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，但被其断然拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其案被阿坝藏族羌族自治州法院秘密庭审，最终在未通知家属旁听的情况下被以“颠覆国家政权罪”、“泄漏国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前在四川省汶川监狱（德阳市黄许镇阿坝监狱或绵阳市川北监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑慈诚（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，藏族良心犯。洛桑慈诚和洛桑祥曲两名年轻僧人于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被当地警方从格尔登寺院抓走后，长达<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月一直没有任何消息。他们被当局指控涉嫌与自焚僧人扎白事件有关。洛桑慈诚，是阿坝县求吉玛乡人，当年<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬被当局秘密（没有通知家属情况下）判处<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">洛桑次仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县格德寺僧人，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在阿坝县城街道上，手持一幅达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，呼喊着“嘉瓦丹增嘉措万岁”疾步行走，独自游街表达了对达赖喇嘛尊者的虔诚信仰，随后被中共公安人员控制带走。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑丹增（藏<span lang="EN-US">/</span>左贡寺高僧）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年左右出生，西藏自治区昌都市左贡县旺达镇乌雅村人，又称乌雅•朱古（即转世喇嘛）洛桑丹增仁波切，早年曾在阿里地区任职导游和司机，后成为西藏左贡寺高僧。曾因经常到西藏的左贡县左贡寺劝导僧俗民众停止供奉所谓的“朵杰凶天”，而要为西藏民族的长远理想和第十四世达赖喇嘛的健康长寿着想，并鼓励藏人努力保护、发扬民族宗教与文化等，受到藏人僧俗的广泛爱戴和尊敬，随招致中共当局的恐慌和严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在西藏拉萨市被左贡县警方抓走刑拘，后被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，被西藏自治区左贡县法院以“追随达赖分裂集团”、“劝诫、蛊惑地方藏民停止修供凶天”等为罪由，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛桑多吉（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1983</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州阿坝县贾柯河牧场人，阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。自幼在甘孜藏族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺出家为僧，曾因屡次谈论有关涉藏敏感话题而遭四川当局的严控打压；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因政治诉求而遭阿坝县警方抓捕，后被阿坝县法院以不知名罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；近年来，因中共当局加大了对所有藏区僧俗的严管力度，尤其是在阿坝县注入大量维稳经费对所辖网络、电话等通讯管道予以严控，并对藏族寺院及被列为怀疑对象的藏人家中频繁进行“突袭搜查”，故而其亦成为被当局因政治原因而维稳、监控的打击对象；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被阿坝县警方从僧舍中强行带走，并被关押在远离阿坝县的一家看守所内，另有格尔登寺僧人洛桑塔克及阿坝河支寺僧人图巴亦被先后抓捕，自此失联；之后不久，其被阿坝县警方以不具名罪由转正式逮捕，被指控因其曾经“向境外发送文字消息”，故而属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，其案在甘孜藏族自治州阿坝县法院开庭审理，后被一审以不详罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。目前被羁押于四川省阿坝县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑格培（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡第二大队人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，曾因政治诉求于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被当局抓捕并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被提前数月释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，其直到一个月前仍处于下落不明状态，且当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑嘉扬（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝自治州阿坝县僧人，现年<span lang="EN-US">28</span>岁，笔名为“鲁米”的藏人作家，是阿坝县麦尔玛乡第三村人。嘉杨自小在阿坝格德寺出家为僧，几年前遭中共当局从该寺驱逐后，前往色达喇荣五明佛学院等佛教寺院继续修学佛法。因在著作中自由表达观点便于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月遭逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日家人获悉他在两个月前被中共当局指控“泄露国家机密”与“分裂国家”罪非法判处了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半有期徒刑。洛桑嘉杨告诉前去探视的亲属，他从未做过触犯法律的事情，也从未向当局“承认”过什么罪行。现在汶川县某监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑克珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">44</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县贾柯河牧场人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾因政治诉求被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后因当时在狱中受虐严重，导致罹患重病而被提前释放，后经由家人、亲友自筹经费，让其住院长时治疗，才得以转危为安。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其因被指控涉嫌“在微信建立组群为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿，特别收集长寿祈愿文持诵及持咒数量”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑曲达（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">西藏安多阿坝县格德寺僧人。中共当局最初在阿坝等地开展“爱国爱教”运动时，他就曾表达不满，并在县政府前张贴文字进行抗议，当时被判处了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年徒刑。出狱后于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与当地的和平抗议活动，呼喊出达赖喇嘛返回西藏的诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被中共警方再次抓捕，约一年后被阿坝县中级人民法院指控“煽动分裂国家”、“代领民众开展示威”，遭判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，现在四川省绵阳监狱中服刑，近日获悉其身体健康状况出现严重问题。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑桑杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，青海省果洛州久治县人，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺（又译格德寺）僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因向外透露格尔登寺僧人自焚抗议事件真相，而被中共当地警方抓捕、刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，并被追加指控涉嫌制作、出售达赖喇嘛的相片和讲法的影片等，违法了中国法律，遂于当年被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日秘密获释；据悉，其在狱中因遭受酷刑虐待，以致出狱时身体状况极差，出现丧失记忆症状；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其再次被当地警方以涉嫌藏人自焚抗议等“政治问题”抓捕、刑拘；在非法关押长达<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月之后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院一审以“政治问题”（不知名罪名）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日；因当地对藏族群体高压严控情况十分严重，故其具体情况缺详。目前其羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛桑坦凯（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿坝县格尔登寺僧人。他<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁。他自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，也是曾被中国当局关闭的寺属学校“佛学青年文苑”第三届毕业生，被捕前在格尔登寺辩经学院中观班就读。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被捕，具体日期不详。洛桑坦凯于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被当局判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。除此之外，有关他被指控的罪名、被关押的地点等情况，因为当局过度的言行限制及网络审查而无法进一步了解。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县安斗乡克洼村人，当地知名画家东阔之子，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因政治诉求而被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被警方带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗保军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗翠琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。罗翠琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗桂友</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，家住广州市增城区，因传播法轮功被中共迫害法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被增城公安局和增城区新塘镇白石派出所警察抓捕。罗桂友被劫入广州市越秀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，罗桂友被白石派出所警察构陷到海珠区检察院。罗桂友于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52187641"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗建荣：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52187641;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗巧俐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，罗巧俐和罗巧萍同时在各自的居住处被抓捕。因为全家修炼法轮功，一直和父母住在一起的弟弟罗晓星及母亲也同时被抓捕。一直被关押在仁和区棉纱湾看守所。姐弟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两次被开庭，后获悉，罗巧俐、罗巧萍、罗晓星分别诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两次被开庭，后获悉，罗巧俐、罗巧萍、罗晓星分别诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">罗让才让（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年生，四川省阿坝县牧民。中共当局指控其叔叔罗让贡求长期与境外藏独组织“格尔底寺新闻联络小组”成员三木旦保持密切联系，罗让贡求单独或者同其侄子罗让才让一起鼓动自焚并将自焚信息提供给三木旦，一些境外媒体利用这些信息进行分裂主义宣传。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日罗让才让被四川警察抓走，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日四川阿坝中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处罗让才让有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">罗让贡求（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，四川省阿坝县格尔登寺僧人；中共当局指控罗让贡求长期与境外藏独组织“格尔底寺新闻联络小组”成员三木旦保持密切联系，罗让贡求单独或者同其侄子罗让才让一起鼓动自焚并将自焚信息提供给三木旦，一些境外媒体利用这些信息进行分裂主义宣传。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日罗让贡求被四川警察抓走，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日四川阿坝中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处罗让贡求死缓，剥夺政治权利终身。现音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，罗巧俐和罗巧萍同时在各自的居住处被抓捕。因为全家修炼法轮功，一直和父母住在一起的弟弟罗晓星及母亲也同时被抓捕。一直被关押在仁和区棉纱湾看守所。姐弟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两次被开庭，后获悉，罗巧俐、罗巧萍、罗晓星分别诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并处罚金。罗晓星刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">骆雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川古蔺县古蔺镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，法轮功学员周糢珍和骆雪梅在习水县醒民镇钢铁村，告诉百姓法轮功真相，被举报。醒民镇派出所抓捕了周糢珍和骆雪梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，周糢珍和骆雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吕耿松：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，浙江省杭州市人，前浙江省高等公安专科学校教师，独立撰稿人，中国民主党浙江委员会重要成员，人权活动家，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日因言获罪被抄家拘捕，并被羁押于浙江省杭州市西湖看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被杭州市中级人民法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日刑满获释。出狱后因仍持守民主理念，关注民主宪政建设，帮助访民维权，遂遭到中共当局严密监控和恶意打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被杭州市警方抄家、传唤；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被杭州市警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被杭州市检察院转正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被杭州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬经浙江省杭州市高级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。目前在浙江省湖州市长湖监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕国妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕国妹是上海浦东新区唐镇前进村西李家宅<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号吕湘福的女儿，他家的合法私有房屋在家庭人员坚守在屋顶护家园抗强拆<span lang="EN-US">6</span>天<span lang="EN-US">5</span>夜半，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">12</span>时许被中共政府强拆。参与护家园抗强拆的今年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁的吕湘福，<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚上被警察带走，同时被带走的另外<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名屋顶抗争者都下落不明。后吕国妹的家属收到《拘留通知书》才知道吕国妹已于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日<span lang="EN-US">19</span>：<span lang="EN-US">55</span>分被上海市公安局浦东分局以“拒不执行判决罪”为名刑事拘留，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所。现音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕先三：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，安徽省淮南市寿县人，曾任小学教师，私营企业职员，执业律师，中国在押维权人士。早年曾就读于安徽省六安师范学校小学教育专业，毕业后曾先在淮南市某镇小学任教，后又在一家私营企业工作<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年始，从事与法律相关的工作，并在安徽省一家律师事务所实习，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年后成为执业律师；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">执业期间，曾至少代理过<span lang="EN-US">80</span>余起案件，其中虽不乏盗窃、诈骗等刑事案件，但大多数属劳动争议纠纷、合同纠纷等民事案件；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，曾经人介绍认识了徐维琴、邵柏春夫妇，并为其及其亲属成功代理了两起借贷纠纷案，受到委托人好评与信任，随于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月起，又受徐维琴等人之委托，陆续代理了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>起民间借贷案；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年前后，因上述民间借贷案的委托人（徐维琴、邵柏春等数人）被合肥市警方以涉黑团伙认定为有预谋的“套路贷”诈骗案，且定为主犯，而其因与徐、邵等委托人之间存有律师代理关系，亦被警方强制定性为该案从犯；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，徐、邵夫妇及其亲友等多人被合肥市警方悉数以涉嫌诈骗案及涉嫌组织、领导、参加黑社会性质组织罪拘捕，其亦于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被合肥市警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其案件被合肥市检察院移交至合肥市中级法院，指控徐维琴、邵柏春等一行多人专门从事非法高利放贷、讨债等活动，利用套路贷侵占他人财物，因而涉嫌犯“组织、领导、参加黑社会性质组织罪以及诈骗罪、敲诈勒索罪、寻衅滋事罪”等，涉案诈骗金额合计逾<span lang="EN-US">1.1</span>亿元，而其作为借贷案代理律师也定于被控告之列；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被合肥市中级法院一审以“诈骗罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万元；其不服判决，立刻提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，经安徽省高级法院二审裁决，因其此前被指有罪的供述笔录是在刑讯逼供的状态下形成，与事实不符，故此二审最终仍以“诈骗罪”改判刑期为有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日；据悉，因其始终坚称无罪，遂对二审宣判依然不服，表示要继续申诉；又悉，其在庭审现场声称在看守所受审讯时曾被酷刑折磨，与其同案的另一主犯（邵柏春）亦称，在被审讯时因警方强逼他指认吕先三有犯罪事实，遭拒后，也被刑讯逼供。目前吕先三被羁押于合肥市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕月霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕月霞与赵文静、黄金桔、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。后所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。该教会成立于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
</div>
